wikipedia wikidata mismatch - follow wikipedia redirect - for species prefixed tags
species:wikidata and species:wikipedia tags link to a different objects, because species:wikipedia tag points to a redirect that should be followed
Q12004 vs (missing) article redirects from en:Quercus to en:Oak
Skrivareiki - an affected OSM element that may be improved

overpass query usable in JOSM that will load all objects where this specific error is present:
